<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;
tab-stops:28.0pt 56.0pt 84.0pt 112.0pt 140.0pt 168.0pt 196.0pt 224.0pt 3.5in 280.0pt 308.0pt 336.0pt;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-right:75.0pt;tab-stops:28.0pt 56.0pt 84.0pt 112.0pt 140.0pt 168.0pt 196.0pt 224.0pt 3.5in 280.0pt 308.0pt 336.0pt;
mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none'><b><span style='font-family:
"AmpleSoft Light";mso-bidi-font-family:"Al Tarikh";color:black;mso-themecolor:
text1'>(3/18/20)</span></b><span style='font-size:16.0pt;font-family:"AmpleSoft Light";
mso-bidi-font-family:"Al Tarikh";color:black;mso-themecolor:text1'> </span><span
style='font-family:"AmpleSoft Light";mso-bidi-font-family:"Al Tarikh";
color:black;mso-themecolor:text1'>Due to the COVID-19 pandemic, the 2020
edition of this course will focus on addressing COVID-19 prediction,
containment, and mitigation <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-right:112.5pt;tab-stops:28.0pt 56.0pt 84.0pt 112.0pt 140.0pt 168.0pt 196.0pt 224.0pt 3.5in 280.0pt 308.0pt 336.0pt;
mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none'><span style='font-family:"AmpleSoft Light";
mso-bidi-font-family:"Al Tarikh";color:black;mso-themecolor:text1'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>(in addition to covering cancer, depression,
and common diseases), using statistical models and AI methods. <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;
tab-stops:28.0pt 56.0pt 84.0pt 112.0pt 140.0pt 168.0pt 196.0pt 224.0pt 3.5in 280.0pt 308.0pt 336.0pt;
mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none'><u><span style='font-size:16.0pt;
font-family:"AmpleSoft Light";mso-bidi-font-family:"Al Tarikh";color:black;
mso-themecolor:text1'><br>
About</span></u><u><span style='font-size:16.0pt;font-family:"AmpleSoft Light";
mso-bidi-font-family:"Al Tarikh";color:white;mso-themecolor:background1'><o:p></o:p></span></u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-right:3.5in;text-align:justify;text-justify:
inter-ideograph;tab-stops:28.0pt 56.0pt 84.0pt 112.0pt 140.0pt 168.0pt 196.0pt 224.0pt 3.5in 280.0pt 308.0pt 336.0pt;
mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none'><span style='font-family:"AmpleSoft Light";
mso-bidi-font-family:"Al Tarikh";color:gray;mso-themecolor:background1;
mso-themeshade:128'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-right:3.5in;text-align:justify;text-justify:
inter-ideograph;tab-stops:28.0pt 56.0pt 84.0pt 112.0pt 140.0pt 168.0pt 196.0pt 224.0pt 3.5in 280.0pt 308.0pt 336.0pt;
mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none'><span style='font-family:"AmpleSoft Light";
mso-bidi-font-family:"Al Tarikh";color:black'><span style='mso-tab-count:1'>      </span>Artificial
intelligence, specifically deep learning, stands out as one of the most
transformative technologies</span><span style='font-family:"Cambria",serif;
mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;color:black'>&nbsp;</span><span style='font-family:
"AmpleSoft Light";mso-bidi-font-family:"Al Tarikh";color:black'>of</span><span
style='font-family:"Cambria",serif;mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;color:black'>&nbsp;</span><span
style='font-family:"AmpleSoft Light";mso-bidi-font-family:"Al Tarikh";
color:black'>the past decade. AI can already outperform humans in several
computer vision and natural language processing tasks.</span><span
style='font-family:"Cambria",serif;mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;color:black'>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span
style='font-family:"AmpleSoft Light";mso-bidi-font-family:"Al Tarikh";
color:black'>However,</span><span style='font-family:"Cambria",serif;
mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;color:black'>&nbsp;</span><span style='font-family:
"AmpleSoft Light";mso-bidi-font-family:"Al Tarikh";color:black'>we still face
some of the same limitations and obstacles</span><span style='font-family:"Cambria",serif;
mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;color:black'>&nbsp;</span><span style='font-family:
"AmpleSoft Light";mso-bidi-font-family:"Al Tarikh";color:black'>that led to the
demise of the first AI boom phase five decades ago.</span><span
style='font-family:"Cambria",serif;mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;color:black'>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span
style='font-family:"AmpleSoft Light";mso-bidi-font-family:"Al Tarikh";
color:black'>This research-oriented course will first review</span><span
style='font-family:"Cambria",serif;mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;color:black'>&nbsp;</span><span
style='font-family:"AmpleSoft Light";mso-bidi-font-family:"Al Tarikh";
color:black'>and reveal the limitations (e.g., <span class=SpellE>iid</span>
assumption on training and testing data, voluminous training data requirement,
and lacking interpretability) of some</span><span style='font-family:"Cambria",serif;
mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;color:black'>&nbsp;</span><span style='font-family:
"AmpleSoft Light";mso-bidi-font-family:"Al Tarikh";color:black'>widely used AI
algorithms, including convolutional neural networks (CNNs), transformers,
reinforcement learning, and generative adversarial networks (GANs). To</span><span
style='font-family:"Cambria",serif;mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;color:black'>&nbsp;</span><span
style='font-family:"AmpleSoft Light";mso-bidi-font-family:"Al Tarikh";
color:black'>address these limitations, we will</span><span style='font-family:
"Cambria",serif;mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;color:black'>&nbsp;</span><span
style='font-family:"AmpleSoft Light";mso-bidi-font-family:"Al Tarikh";
color:black'>then</span><span style='font-family:"Cambria",serif;mso-bidi-font-family:
Cambria;color:black'>&nbsp;</span><span style='font-family:"AmpleSoft Light";
mso-bidi-font-family:"Al Tarikh";color:black'>explore topics including transfer
learning</span><span style='font-family:"AmpleSoft Light";mso-bidi-font-family:
"Al Tarikh";color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW'> for remedying data
scarcity</span><span style='font-family:"AmpleSoft Light";mso-bidi-font-family:
"Al Tarikh";color:black'>, knowledge-guided multimodal learning for improving
data diversity, out of distribution generalization, attention mechanisms for
enabling Interpretability, meta learning, and privacy-preserving training data
management.</span><span style='font-family:"Cambria",serif;mso-bidi-font-family:
Cambria;color:black'>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style='font-family:"AmpleSoft Light";
mso-bidi-font-family:"Al Tarikh";color:black'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-right:3.5in;text-align:justify;text-justify:
inter-ideograph;tab-stops:28.0pt 56.0pt 84.0pt 112.0pt 140.0pt 168.0pt 196.0pt 224.0pt 3.5in 280.0pt 308.0pt 336.0pt;
mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none'><span style='font-family:"AmpleSoft Light";
mso-bidi-font-family:"Al Tarikh";color:black'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-right:3.5in;text-align:justify;text-justify:
inter-ideograph;tab-stops:28.0pt 56.0pt 84.0pt 112.0pt 140.0pt 168.0pt 196.0pt 224.0pt 3.5in 280.0pt 308.0pt 336.0pt;
mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none'><span style='font-family:"AmpleSoft Light";
mso-bidi-font-family:"Al Tarikh";color:black'>The course will be taught through
a combination of lecture and project sessions. Lectures on specialized AI
applications (e.g., cancer/depression diagnosis and treatment, AI/VR for
surgery, and </span><span style='font-family:"AmpleSoft Light";mso-bidi-font-family:
"Al Tarikh";color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW'>health </span><span
style='font-family:"AmpleSoft Light";mso-bidi-font-family:"Al Tarikh";
color:black'>education) will feature guest speakers from academia and industry.
Students will be assigned to work on an extensive project that is relevant to
their fields of study (e.g., CS, Medicine, and Data Science). Projects may
involve conducting literature surveys, formulating ideas, and implementing
these ideas. Example project topics are but not limited to 1) knowledge guided
GANs for improving training data diversity, 2) disease diagnosis via multimodal
symptom checking, and 3) methods for COVID-19 path prediction and immunity
analysis.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-right:3.5in;text-align:justify;text-justify:
inter-ideograph;tab-stops:28.0pt 56.0pt 84.0pt 112.0pt 140.0pt 168.0pt 196.0pt 224.0pt 3.5in 280.0pt 308.0pt 336.0pt;
mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none'><span style='font-family:"AmpleSoft Light";
mso-bidi-font-family:"Al Tarikh";color:black'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph'><span
style='font-family:"AmpleSoft Light";mso-bidi-font-family:"Al Tarikh";
color:black;mso-themecolor:text1;background:white'>Level: CS senior/graduate,
proficient in programming<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph'><span
